## Diagram 1

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    A[useOrganizations called] --> B[Extract ids and fvIds from props]
    B --> C[Filter and transform ids/fvIds]
    C --> D[Create getLatestIds and getLatestFvIds]
    D --> E[Stringify ids for effect dependency]
    E --> F{useEffect triggered}
    F --> G[Get latest ids and fvIds]
    G --> H{ids or fvIds exist?}
    H -->|Yes| I[dispatch fetchOrganizations]
    H -->|No| J[Skip fetch]
    I --> K[useSelector for orgsByDbId]
    J --> K
    K --> L[useSelector for orgsByFvId]
    L --> M[Create getOrganizationByDbId callback]
    M --> N[Create getOrganizationByFvId callback]
    N --> O[Return hook interface with callbacks and isLoading]
```

## Diagram 2

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Component
    participant useOrganizations
    participant useGetLatest
    participant useEffect
    participant Redux
    participant useSelector
    
    Component->>useOrganizations: Call with ids/fvIds
    useOrganizations->>useGetLatest: Create getLatestIds
    useOrganizations->>useGetLatest: Create getLatestFvIds
    useOrganizations->>useEffect: Trigger effect
    useEffect->>useGetLatest: getLatestIds()
    useEffect->>useGetLatest: getLatestFvIds()
    useEffect->>Redux: dispatch(fetchOrganizations)
    Redux-->>useEffect: Action dispatched
    useOrganizations->>useSelector: getOrganizationByDbId
    useSelector-->>useOrganizations: orgsByDbId
    useOrganizations->>useSelector: getOrganizationByFvId
    useSelector-->>useOrganizations: orgsByFvId
    useOrganizations->>Component: Return callbacks and isLoading
```
